Berkeley High is an incredible school with amazing resources and opportunities. There are classes for practically everything, and students can be as challenged as they want. We have over 80 clubs, an award winning newspaper and jazz program, and not to mention a ridiculous number of hilarious and fun traditions (RALLY DAY, Assassin, Senior Streak, promposals, Dare Night). I‚Äôm so grateful for Berkeley High and the wonderful people here.</Review>

I a teacher from Upstate NY and know the true example of the quality of a school is when neither teacher or parents are around.  I was at several different stores and each time met students from Berkeley.  They were Polite and Helpful. I come from a  rural part of NY so not used to a big city school system>  I am impressed by the students behavior and willingness to help.  They enjoyed talking sports during the process as well - not a surprise having been a coach.  I came to CA to be a Grad Student. I will be less hesitant to look into being a Sub for this district by their students' example when neither parent or teacher is around. I never stepped foot on the campus, but I am impressed by  these students actions. It is not what is said is important, but how their actions speak it!  My compliments to all of you.  Now one encouraged me to try my hand at skate boarding, but chose not to try, I nearly broke bones when I said this looked easy till I placed the second foot on the board.   Hey, Keep up the Great work!<//review>

< text>
I know that there are a multitude of outstanding teachers at BHS, but the student body is so large that you will rarely get one. Instead, you will spend most of your high school career with teachers who, even in their prime, have never been more than mediocre. Not to mention the near incompetent administration and severe grade gap. In fact, there is no support for students who are simply average.</text>

< Review>
I needed some small acrylic label blocks for my mineral collection. There are lots of blocks out there but all are suited more for retail commercial displays  and thus far too large, clunky or expensive. Found ePlastics on the web and thought that some of their 0.5" acrylic rod would do the trick if sliced into small pieces. Orders always come in on time and when I've had questions concerning a product someone always picks up the phone at ePlastics.  They also offer a wider range of Plexiglass products, especially the thickness of the Plexi, that is hard to find anywhere else.  I'm on the East Coast, and the packaging/shipping is a concern with Plexiglas orders.  ePlastics packs the glass really well and I've never had a piece delivered with a crack or even a scratch.  I highly recommend ePlastics and feel they do a great job!<//Text>

I've been a reluctant Ridout customer off and on since the 60's. Sometimes they have what I want at a price which is too high, but which I'm willing to pay because I want it now. But from day 1 their attitude toward customers, especially ones who don't look like they are going to be spending a lot of money, is uniformly abusive. The overall attitude is "hey buddy, this isn't a lumber company, this is PLASTIC". The fabrication quality is usually good, but the attitude toward customers and the way they run the store is bad. Avoid.</Text>

Food: I saw they had posted a picture of their waffle sandwich and I had to try it! I had the waffle fish sandwich. The waffle was made fresh and had a natural sweetness to it. The fish was battered but not too heavy. It also had coleslaw and was topped with a chipotle aioli sauce. It wound up being more of a taco shape than sandwich but either way it was delicious. I ordered grilled veggies on the side, they were grilled with garlic, which I appreciated. My little sister had the fish and chips, she devoured it, so I think she liked it lol!

Drinks: We didn't get too adventurous with the drinks today. Just stuck to the fountain beverages.

Setting: Clean, with tables and a couple of bar tops. The walls are a calming blue and there's a pair of wings painted on one side that make for an excellent photo op.

Service: Fast and friendly.

Verdict: I'll definitely be back to explore more of the menu.< /text>

< Review>
Bottom line, great food and service. Very pleasing atmosphere. The aroma of barbeque, along with high spirits made my first time here enjoyable. Parking doesn't seem bad, menu is very easy to understand. There was a female cashier who greeted/helped my group, and the owner's son was a big help as well- both friendly.

Loved the aesthetic of the place, very clean and plenty of room.
I ordered a Tasha's trio which includes: 3 sandwiches. One containing chicken, pulled pork, and the last brisket. I had a side of coleslaw. My friends got some meat and salad

They were all delicious sandwichs, but the one top the rest was that smokey, succulent brisket. That white bread with mouthwatering BBQ slathered on tender brisket?! You guys are killing it! üíØ  Next time I go, which surley I will, best believe I'm going to get that brisket. Thanks for the hard work.  üëçüèº

<rate>5< /rate><Review>This an awesome place to experience great barbecue made by hard working salt of the earth people!  I am talking about real food, like fresh baked beans stewed with chunks of barbecued pork, not canned.  The Coleslaw was fresh, and I loved the celery seed seasoning to give it that extra fresh flavor.  And the barbecue...well, you'll have to experience the tender fall apart brisket and flavorful ribs. < Review>
I'm a fan.  Not the 'greatest' per say but still some really kind grinds.
I went with a friend and she recommended that I try the "Beef Brisket Sandwich" (sliced brisket, BBQ sauce, red onion and a sliced pickle on a French roll). @  $7.80
Instead I decided to order the "Pork Loin Sandwich" (sliced pork, BBQ sauce, onion, a sliced pickle on a French roll).@  $7.80
We split the Blake's Rings and French Fries combo: @ $5

So the experience we had was that this place was pretty crowded.  There was this guy sporting the coolest handlebar mustache; which I haven't seen in a long time. He took our order. We sat outside and our order came out rather quickly. The food runner was way nice and friendly.  While we were approximately half way through our meal another food runner going table to table asking about our experience.
Environment wise: Pretty cool: Plenty of seating inside and on the patio. TV's were set to sports channels and staff was super friendly.
Food wise: The  "Pork Loin Sandwich" was way to dry and I had to add BBQ sauce to help try and wet it up. Might've came in to order this on the wrong day.
Thank goodness I gave half of my sandwich to my friend and she gave me half of hers.  Her sandwich was GREAT!  I should've listened to her : /
The Onion Rings and French Fries were good.  The Onions rings were better since the fries came out a bit on the dry side and had to try and salvage them by the savior known as "Ketchup"

So here it is in a nutshell: Try the "Beef Brisket Sandwich"<//Review>

<UserId.>105692744256480109238</UserId.><name>Chelsea Madren (OC Food Diva)<//name><Time>1334452744126</Time><rating>4</rating>< Text>
The Pulled Pork is exactly what it sounds like. It‚Äôs tender, slow-cooked, smoked pork that literally falls apart into shreds. They toss it in Blake‚Äôs BBQ sauce and serve it up in a lump. It has a little too much BBQ sauce for me. I‚Äôm more of a smoked meat person who uses the sauce on the side to add as needed. Otherwise, the pork tasted pretty good. Thumbs up!

Blake‚Äôs Big Pulled Pork Pile is slow smoked pork, pulled and served on their big bun with BBQ sauce, cole slaw, and red onion. You‚Äôll definitely need extra napkins for this sandwich! Again, a little too much BBQ sauce for me, but my family loved this sandwich! The sweet, BBQ sauced smoky pork complemented the cool, creamy cole slaw. The bun was soft yet held this pork beast together. Thumbs up! If you‚Äôre feeling a bit of Man vs. Food hunger, they also offer the Blake‚Äôs One Pounder Bomber or ‚ÄúTHE BEAST‚Äù (two and a half pounds of food, YIKES!)

Sandy‚Äôs Bread Pudding is a huge portion with a side of vanilla sauce to slather on. It was a very dense and custardy bread pudding. It had a bit more raisins in it than expected. The vanilla sauce was creamy and gave it a down-home comfy goodness. Thumbs up!</Text>
